### [1] [RoboLayout: Differentiable 3D Scene Generation for Embodied Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05522)
*Ali Shamsaddinlou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出RoboLayout，一个用于生成适合具身智能体交互的3D室内场景布局的模型，通过引入可达性约束和局部优化改进了现有模型。该模型支持多种具身智能体，并提高了场景布局的可导航性和可操作性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型在生成3D场景布局时，虽然语义上连贯，但在物理上可交互性方面存在挑战，尤其是在室内环境中，难以生成适合具身智能体（如机器人、人类）交互的场景。

Method: RoboLayout扩展了LayoutVLM模型，引入了具身智能体感知的推理能力和优化的稳定性。它将显式的可达性约束融入到可微分的布局优化过程中，并增加了一个局部精调阶段，用于选择性地重新优化有问题的物体放置，从而提高收敛效率。

Result: RoboLayout在保持LayoutVLM的语义对齐和物理合理性的同时，显著增强了其在以智能体为中心的室内场景生成方面的应用性。实验结果表明，该模型能生成适合不同智能体（服务机器人、仓储机器人、不同年龄段的人类等）的、可导航且可操作的室内场景布局。

Conclusion: RoboLayout成功地解决了在室内环境中为具身智能体生成可交互场景布局的挑战，通过引入具身智能体感知和优化策略，提高了生成场景的可行性和实用性，并展示了其跨平台和跨智能体的通用性。

Abstract: Recent advances in vision language models (VLMs) have shown strong potential for spatial reasoning and 3D scene layout generation from open-ended language instructions. However, generating layouts that are not only semantically coherent but also feasible for interaction by embodied agents remains challenging, particularly in physically constrained indoor environments. In this paper, RoboLayout is introduced as an extension of LayoutVLM that augments the original framework with agent-aware reasoning and improved optimization stability. RoboLayout integrates explicit reachability constraints into a differentiable layout optimization process, enabling the generation of layouts that are navigable and actionable by embodied agents. Importantly, the agent abstraction is not limited to a specific robot platform and can represent diverse entities with distinct physical capabilities, such as service robots, warehouse robots, humans of different age groups, or animals, allowing environment design to be tailored to the intended agent. In addition, a local refinement stage is proposed that selectively reoptimizes problematic object placements while keeping the remainder of the scene fixed, improving convergence efficiency without increasing global optimization iterations. Overall, RoboLayout preserves the strong semantic alignment and physical plausibility of LayoutVLM while enhancing applicability to agent-centric indoor scene generation, as demonstrated by experimental results across diverse scene configurations.

</details>


### [2] [Reasoning Models Struggle to Control their Chains of Thought](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05706)
*Chen Yueh-Han,Robert McCarthy,Bruce W. Lee,He He,Ian Kivlichan,Bowen Baker,Micah Carroll,Tomek Korbak*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究引入了CoT-Control评估套件，用于衡量大型语言模型控制其思考链（CoT）输出的能力。结果表明，模型在控制CoT方面能力较弱，但如果能被利用，可能仍会构成CoT可监控性的风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着CoT监控技术的发展，研究者担心模型可能控制其CoT输出，从而削弱CoT监控的效果。因此，需要量化模型控制其CoT的能力，以评估CoT监控的可靠性。

Method: 引入CoT-Control评估套件，包含需要模型在特定CoT约束下解决问题的任务。通过实验比较模型在控制CoT输出和最终输出方面的能力，并分析模型规模、RL训练、计算量、问题难度、监控奖励和对抗性提示等因素对CoT可控性的影响。

Result: 大型语言模型在控制CoT方面的能力远低于控制最终输出的能力。例如，Claude Sonnet 4.5在控制CoT方面仅有2.7%的成功率，而在控制最终输出方面则有61.9%。CoT可控性随模型规模增大而提高，随RL训练、测试时间计算量和问题难度增加而降低。即使有监控奖励，模型也仅略微提高可控性，对抗性提示也未能显著提升。

Conclusion: 目前来看，模型操纵其CoT输出以规避监控的可能性较低，CoT可控性不太可能成为CoT可监控性的主要失效模式。然而，低可控性的具体机制尚不明确。鉴于其对CoT可监控性的重要性，建议相关研究机构在未来模型开发中监测CoT可控性。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring is a promising tool for detecting misbehaviors and understanding the motivations of modern reasoning models. However, if models can control what they verbalize in their CoT, it could undermine CoT monitorability. To measure this undesirable capability -- CoT controllability -- we introduce the CoT-Control evaluation suite, which includes tasks that require models to solve problems while adhering to CoT instructions, e.g., reasoning about a genetics question without using the word 'chromosome'. We show that reasoning models possess significantly lower CoT controllability than output controllability; for instance, Claude Sonnet 4.5 can control its CoT only 2.7% of the time but 61.9% when controlling its final output. We also find that CoT controllability is higher for larger models and decreases with more RL training, test-time compute, and increased problem difficulty. CoT controllability failures extend even to situations in which models are given incentives (as opposed to direct requests) to evade CoT monitors, although models exhibit slightly higher controllability when they are told they are being monitored. Similarly, eliciting controllability by adversarially optimizing prompts does not meaningfully increase controllability. Our results leave us cautiously optimistic that CoT controllability is currently unlikely to be a failure mode of CoT monitorability. However, the mechanism behind low controllability is not well understood. Given its importance for maintaining CoT monitorability, we recommend that frontier labs track CoT controllability in future models.

</details>


### [3] [Real-Time AI Service Economy: A Framework for Agentic Computing Across the Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05614)
*Lauri Lovén,Alaa Saleh,Reza Farahani,Ilir Murturi,Miguel Bordallo López,Praveen Kumar Donta,Schahram Dustdar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究表明，在设备-边缘-云连续体上运行的实时 AI 服务，其服务依赖图的结构（DAG）是去中心化、基于价格的资源分配能否大规模可靠工作的关键因素。研究提出了一个混合管理架构，以解决复杂依赖关系导致的资源分配问题，并验证了该架构在价格稳定性和吞吐量方面优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 AI 服务越来越多地部署在设备-边缘-云连续体中，这些服务产生了复杂的、对延迟敏感的工作负载，并需要资源协调。研究旨在了解服务依赖图结构如何影响基于价格的去中心化资源分配的可行性和效率，并提出一种解决方案来应对复杂依赖关系带来的挑战。

Method: 研究使用服务依赖图（DAG）来建模计算阶段及其执行顺序。通过理论分析和实验来研究价格的收敛性、最优分配的可计算性以及激励机制。对于复杂的依赖关系，提出了一个混合管理架构，其中跨域集成器将复杂的子图封装为资源切片，从而简化了市场接口。并通过一项涉及六个实验、1620 次运行和 10 种随机种子（seeds）的消融研究来验证该架构。

Result: 研究发现，当依赖图具有层次结构（树形或串并联）时，价格会收敛到稳定的均衡，最优分配可以高效计算，并且在合适的机制设计下，代理没有动机进行虚假报价。然而，当依赖关系更复杂时，价格会出现波动，分配质量下降。混合管理架构可以将价格波动降低 70-75%，同时不牺牲吞吐量。治理约束会导致可量化的效率-合规性权衡。在真实报价的情况下，去中心化市场可以达到与集中式最优基线相媲美的分配质量。

Conclusion: 服务依赖图的拓扑结构是影响去中心化资源分配稳定性和可扩展性的首要因素。研究提出的混合管理架构能够有效地解决复杂依赖关系带来的挑战，提高资源分配的效率和稳定性。去中心化协调能够在保持效率的同时，复制集中式分配的质量。

Abstract: Real-time AI services increasingly operate across the device-edge-cloud continuum, where autonomous AI agents generate latency-sensitive workloads, orchestrate multi-stage processing pipelines, and compete for shared resources under policy and governance constraints. This article shows that the structure of service-dependency graphs, modelled as DAGs whose nodes represent compute stages and whose edges encode execution ordering, is a primary determinant of whether decentralised, price-based resource allocation can work reliably at scale. When dependency graphs are hierarchical (tree or series-parallel), prices converge to stable equilibria, optimal allocations can be computed efficiently, and under appropriate mechanism design (with quasilinear utilities and discrete slice items), agents have no incentive to misreport their valuations within each decision epoch. When dependencies are more complex, with cross-cutting ties between pipeline stages, prices oscillate, allocation quality degrades, and the system becomes difficult to manage. To bridge this gap, we propose a hybrid management architecture in which cross-domain integrators encapsulate complex sub-graphs into resource slices that present a simpler, well-structured interface to the rest of the market. A systematic ablation study across six experiments (1,620 runs, 10 seeds each) confirms that (i) dependency-graph topology is a first-order determinant of price stability and scalability,(ii) the hybrid architecture reduces price volatility by up to 70-75% without sacrificing throughput, (iii) governance constraints create quantifiable efficiency-compliance trade-offs that depend jointly on topology and load, and (iv) under truthful bidding the decentralised market matches a centralised value-optimal baseline, confirming that decentralised coordination can replicate centralised allocation quality.

</details>


### [4] [Evolving Medical Imaging Agents via Experience-driven Self-skill Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05860)
*Lin Fan,Pengyu Dai,Zhipeng Deng,Haolin Wang,Xun Gong,Yefeng Zheng,Yafei Ou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为MACRO的自适应医疗AI代理，它能通过学习有效的工具使用序列并将其合成为新的复合工具，从而持续优化多步骤医学图像解读任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于LLM的医疗AI代理在工具集和调用策略上是静态的，这使得它们在面对真实世界的领域变化、新任务或不断发展的诊断需求时表现脆弱，需要昂贵的手动重新设计。研究旨在克服这种静态工具组合的局限性。

Method: MACRO通过以下方式实现自我进化：1. 从已验证的执行轨迹中自动识别有效的多步骤工具序列；2. 将这些序列合成为可重用的复合工具；3. 将新发现的复合工具注册为高级原语，不断扩展代理的能力；4. 利用轻量级的图像特征记忆来结合视觉和临床上下文；5. 采用类似GRPO的训练循环，通过少量监督来强化对新复合工具的可靠调用，实现闭环自我改进。

Result: 在多个医学影像数据集和任务上的实验表明，MACRO通过自主发现复合工具，在多步骤任务的协调准确性和跨领域泛化能力上，持续优于现有的基线方法和最新的AI代理方法。

Conclusion: MACRO通过一种经验驱动的工具发现机制，实现了医疗AI代理在多步骤任务中的自适应性和鲁棒性，显著提高了性能并缩小了静态工具使用与自适应、上下文感知型临床AI助手之间的差距。

Abstract: Clinical image interpretation is inherently multi-step and tool-centric: clinicians iteratively combine visual evidence with patient context, quantify findings, and refine their decisions through a sequence of specialized procedures. While LLM-based agents promise to orchestrate such heterogeneous medical tools, existing systems treat tool sets and invocation strategies as static after deployment. This design is brittle under real-world domain shifts, across tasks, and evolving diagnostic requirements, where predefined tool chains frequently degrade and demand costly manual re-design. We propose MACRO, a self-evolving, experience-augmented medical agent that shifts from static tool composition to experience-driven tool discovery. From verified execution trajectories, the agent autonomously identifies recurring effective multi-step tool sequences, synthesizes them into reusable composite tools, and registers these as new high-level primitives that continuously expand its behavioral repertoire. A lightweight image-feature memory grounds tool selection in a visual-clinical context, while a GRPO-like training loop reinforces reliable invocation of discovered composites, enabling closed-loop self-improvement with minimal supervision. Extensive experiments across diverse medical imaging datasets and tasks demonstrate that autonomous composite tool discovery consistently improves multi-step orchestration accuracy and cross-domain generalization over strong baselines and recent state-of-the-art agentic methods, bridging the gap between brittle static tool use and adaptive, context-aware clinical AI assistance. Code will be available upon acceptance.

</details>


### [5] [The World Won't Stay Still: Programmable Evolution for Agent Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05910)
*Guangrui Li,Yaochen Xie,Yi Liu,Ziwei Dong,Xingyuan Pan,Tianqi Zheng,Jason Choi,Michael J. Morais,Binit Jha,Shaunak Mishra,Bingrou Zhou,Chen Luo,Monica Xiao Cheng,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为ProEvolve的基于图的框架，用于以可控且可扩展的方式演化LLM代理的环境，以评估代理的适应性。该框架通过类型化关系图来统一表示环境（数据、工具、模式），并将环境的演化表示为图变换，从而实现环境的自动化生成和任务沙盒的实例化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大多数基准测试都假设环境是静态的，并且模式和工具集是固定的，这忽略了现实世界中环境的演变性质以及代理对环境变化的鲁棒性。因此，研究如何以可扩展和可控的方式演化代理环境，以更好地评估代理对真实世界动态的适应性，具有重要意义。

Method: 提出了一种名为ProEvolve的基于图的框架。核心是一个类型化关系图，它提供了一个统一的、显式的环境表示（数据、工具、模式）。在此形式化下，添加、删除或修改能力被表示为图变换，这些变换在工具、模式和数据访问之间进行连贯的更新传播。ProEvolve能够通过图变换编程环境的演化动态以自动生成环境，并通过子图采样和编程实例化任务沙盒。

Result: 通过ProEvolve，成功地将一个环境演化成200个环境和3000个任务沙盒，并对代表性代理进行了相应基准测试。

Conclusion: ProEvolve是一个可编程的框架，能够以可扩展和可控的方式演化LLM代理的环境，从而为评估代理的适应性提供了一个更现实的测试平台。

Abstract: LLM-powered agents fulfill user requests by interacting with environments, querying data, and invoking tools in a multi-turn process. Yet, most existing benchmarks assume static environments with fixed schemas and toolsets, neglecting the evolutionary nature of the real world and agents' robustness to environmental changes. In this paper, we study a crucial problem: how to evolve the agent environment in a scalable and controllable way, thereby better evaluating agents' adaptability to real-world dynamics. We propose ProEvolve, a graph-based framework that makes environment evolution programmable. At its core, a typed relational graph provides a unified, explicit representation of the environment: data, tools, and schema. Under this formalism, adding, removing, or modifying capabilities are expressed as graph transformations that coherently propagate updates across tools, schemas, and data access. Building on this, ProEvolve can (1) program the evolutionary dynamics as graph transformations to generate environments automatically, and (2) instantiate task sandboxes via subgraph sampling and programming. We validate ProEvolve by evolving a single environment into 200 environments and 3,000 task sandboxes, and benchmark representative agents accordingly.

</details>


### [6] [DeepFact: Co-Evolving Benchmarks and Agents for Deep Research Factuality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05912)
*Yukun Huang,Leonardo F. R. Ribeiro,Momchil Hardalov,Bhuwan Dhingra,Markus Dreyer,Venkatesh Saligrama*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究提出了一种名为Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score (AtS)的新方法，用于构建和评估用于深层研究报告（DRRs）的声明级事实核查基准。该方法通过迭代审计和修订来提高事实核查的准确性，并在此基础上构建了DeepFact-Bench基准和DeepFact-Eval验证剂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的事实核查方法难以验证搜索增强的大型语言模型（LLM）生成的深层研究报告（DRRs）中的声明级事实性，并且缺乏专门针对DRRs的基准测试。研究人员发现，静态专家标注的基准在DRR事实核查任务中表现不佳，准确率仅为60.8%。

Method: 研究人员提出了一种名为Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score (AtS)的新型基准构建方法。在该方法中，当验证器与现有基准标签不一致时，验证器需要提供证据，由审计员裁决争议，并将被接受的修订更新到基准中，然后再对模型进行评分。研究人员基于AtS方法构建了一个名为DeepFact-Bench的版本化DRR事实性基准，以及一个名为DeepFact-Eval的文档级验证剂。

Result: 通过四轮AtS迭代，专家在微型黄金标准数据集上的准确率从60.8%提高到90.9%。DeepFact-Eval验证剂在DeepFact-Bench基准上表现优于现有验证器，并且在外部事实性数据集上也表现出良好的迁移性。

Conclusion: AtS方法能够显著提高事实核查的准确性和可靠性，克服了静态专家标注基准的局限性。DeepFact-Bench和DeepFact-Eval为DRR事实性验证提供了一个有效且可演进的解决方案。

Abstract: Search-augmented LLM agents can produce deep research reports (DRRs), but verifying claim-level factuality remains challenging. Existing fact-checkers are primarily designed for general-domain, factoid-style atomic claims, and there is no benchmark to test whether such verifiers transfer to DRRs. Yet building such a benchmark is itself difficult. We first show that static expert-labeled benchmarks are brittle in this setting: in a controlled study with PhD-level specialists, unassisted experts achieve only 60.8% accuracy on a hidden micro-gold set of verifiable claims. We propose Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score (AtS), where benchmark labels and rationales are explicitly revisable: when a verifier disagrees with the current benchmark, it must submit evidence; an auditor adjudicates the dispute; and accepted revisions update the benchmark before models are scored. Across four AtS rounds, expert micro-gold accuracy rises to 90.9%, indicating experts are substantially more reliable as auditors than as one-shot labelers. We instantiate AtS as DeepFact-Bench, a versioned DRR factuality benchmark with auditable rationales, and DeepFact-Eval, a document-level verification agent (with a grouped lite variant) that outperforms existing verifiers on DeepFact-Bench and transfers well to external factuality datasets.

</details>


### [7] [An Interactive Multi-Agent System for Evaluation of New Product Concepts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05980)
*Bin Xuan,Ruo Ai,Hakyeon Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于大型语言模型（LLM）的多智能体系统（MAS），用于自动化产品概念评估，以克服传统专家评估的主观性和成本问题。该系统通过模拟专业团队，利用检索增强生成（RAG）和实时搜索来评估技术和市场可行性，并在案例研究中证明其评估结果与行业专家一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的产品概念评估依赖专家，存在主观偏见、高成本和耗时的问题，因此需要一种更自动化、客观的支持方法。

Method: 构建了一个包含八个虚拟智能体的LLM-MAS系统，每个智能体代表不同的专业领域。该系统利用检索增强生成（RAG）和实时搜索工具收集客观证据，并基于技术可行性和市场可行性这两个维度进行结构化讨论和评估。智能体还通过专业产品评审数据进行了微调。

Result: 在针对专业显示器概念的案例研究中，所提出的MAS系统的评估排名与资深行业专家的评估结果一致。

Conclusion: 基于多智能体的自动化产品概念评估方法是可行的，能够有效地支持产品开发决策，并有望克服传统方法的局限性。

Abstract: Product concept evaluation is a critical stage that determines strategic resource allocation and project success in enterprises. However, traditional expert-led approaches face limitations such as subjective bias and high time and cost requirements. To support this process, this study proposes an automated approach utilizing a large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent system (MAS). Through a systematic analysis of previous research on product development and team collaboration, this study established two primary evaluation dimensions, namely technical feasibility and market feasibility. The proposed system consists of a team of eight virtual agents representing specialized domains such as R&D and marketing. These agents use retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and real-time search tools to gather objective evidence and validate concepts through structured deliberations based on the established criteria. The agents were further fine-tuned using professional product review data to enhance their judgment accuracy. A case study involving professional display monitor concepts demonstrated that the system's evaluation rankings were consistent with those of senior industry experts. These results confirm the usability of the proposed multi-agent-based evaluation approach for supporting product development decisions.

</details>


### [8] [Agentic LLM Planning via Step-Wise PDDL Simulation: An Empirical Characterisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06064)
*Kai Göbel,Pierrick Lorang,Patrik Zips,Tobias Glück*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个名为 PyPDDLEngine 的开源 PDDL 模拟引擎，它允许大型语言模型（LLM）通过工具调用进行交互式任务规划。实验表明，与传统的规划器 Fast Downward 相比，LLM 规划在 Blocksworld 任务上取得了可比但略低的成功率，并且具有更高的成本。然而，LLM 规划器能够生成更短的计划，这可能归因于训练数据回忆而非泛化规划能力。研究还指出，LLM 在编码任务中获得的收益似乎依赖于外部反馈信号，而在 PDDL 规划中，缺乏此类反馈限制了其进步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大型语言模型（LLM）是否能作为独立的规划器，与经典的符号规划方法相媲美，以及如何利用 LLM 的交互能力来改进规划过程。

Method: 提出并实现了一个名为 PyPDDLEngine 的开源 PDDL 模拟引擎，该引擎通过 Model Context Protocol (MCP) 接口将规划操作暴露为 LLM 的工具调用。LLM 作为一种交互式搜索策略，逐个选择动作，观察状态变化，并能够重置和重试。在 102 个 Blocksworld 实例上，将 Fast Downward（lama-first 和 seq-sat-lama-2011）、直接 LLM 规划（Claude Haiku 4.5）和通过 PyPDDLEngine 的代理式 LLM 规划进行了比较。

Result: 在 180 秒的时间预算下，Fast Downward 实现了 85.3% 的成功率。直接 LLM 规划和代理式 LLM 规划的成功率分别为 63.7% 和 66.7%，代理式方法略有优势（3%），但 token 成本高出 5.7 倍。在共同解决的难度块中，LLM 方法生成的计划比 seq-sat-lama-2011 更短，这可能表明这是训练数据回忆而非泛化规划。

Conclusion: 代理式 LLM 规划在 PDDL 任务中的收益有限，这可能与缺乏外部验证的自我评估式环境反馈有关，而编码代理则受益于编译器错误和测试失败等外部反馈信号。LLM 规划器的优势可能更多地源于训练数据中的模式记忆，而非真正的规划能力。

Abstract: Task planning, the problem of sequencing actions to reach a goal from an initial state, is a core capability requirement for autonomous robotic systems. Whether large language models (LLMs) can serve as viable planners alongside classical symbolic methods remains an open question. We present PyPDDLEngine, an open-source Planning Domain Definition Language (PDDL) simulation engine that exposes planning operations as LLM tool calls through a Model Context Protocol (MCP) interface. Rather than committing to a complete action sequence upfront, the LLM acts as an interactive search policy that selects one action at a time, observes each resulting state, and can reset and retry. We evaluate four approaches on 102 International Planning Competition (IPC) Blocksworld instances under a uniform 180-second budget: Fast Downward lama-first and seq-sat-lama-2011 as classical baselines, direct LLM planning (Claude Haiku 4.5), and agentic LLM planning via PyPDDLEngine. Fast Downward achieves 85.3% success. The direct and agentic LLM approaches achieve 63.7% and 66.7%, respectively, a consistent but modest three-percentage-point advantage for the agentic approach at $5.7\times$ higher token cost per solution. Across most co-solved difficulty blocks, both LLM approaches produce shorter plans than seq-sat-lama-2011 despite its iterative quality improvement, a result consistent with training-data recall rather than generalisable planning. These results suggest that agentic gains depend on the nature of environmental feedback. Coding agents benefit from externally grounded signals such as compiler errors and test failures, whereas PDDL step feedback is self-assessed, leaving the agent to evaluate its own progress without external verification.

</details>


### [9] [Aggregative Semantics for Quantitative Bipolar Argumentation Frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06067)
*Yann Munro,Isabelle Bloch,Marie-Jeanne Lesot*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的定量双极论证框架（QBAF）下的渐进式语义，称为聚合语义。该语义通过分别聚合攻击者和支持者的权重，然后将其与论证本身的权重结合，来处理攻击和支持角色的不对称性，并提供更灵活和可解释的计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理论证框架中的攻击和支持关系时，未能充分考虑攻击者和支持者角色的不对称性。此外，现有的渐进式语义在可解释性和参数化方面仍有改进空间。

Method: 提出了一种三阶段的聚合语义计算方法：1. 分别计算论证的攻击者权重。2. 分别计算论证的支持者权重。3. 将攻击者权重、支持者权重与论证本身的权重进行聚合。讨论了聚合函数应满足的性质，并与经典渐进式语义原则进行比较。通过简单示例和对 500 种聚合语义的测试进行说明。

Result: 开发了一种新的、可参数化的渐进式语义（聚合语义），它能更好地捕捉双极论证框架中的不对称性。通过实验展示了聚合语义行为的多样性。

Conclusion: 聚合语义为定量双极论证框架提供了一种新颖、灵活且可解释的方法，能够处理攻击和支持角色的不对称性，并比现有方法更能保持论证框架的双极特性。

Abstract: Formal argumentation is being used increasingly in artificial intelligence as an effective and understandable way to model potentially conflicting pieces of information, called arguments, and identify so-called acceptable arguments depending on a chosen semantics. This paper deals with the specific context of Quantitative Bipolar Argumentation Frameworks (QBAF), where arguments have intrinsic weights and can attack or support each other. In this context, we introduce a novel family of gradual semantics, called aggregative semantics. In order to deal with situations in which attackers and supporters do not play a symmetric role, and in contrast to modular semantics, we propose to aggregate attackers and supporters separately. This leads to a three-stage computation, which consists in computing a global weight for attackers and another for supporters, before aggregating these two values with the intrinsic weight of the argument. We discuss the properties that the three aggregation functions should satisfy depending on the context, as well as their relationships with the classical principles for gradual semantics. This discussion is supported by various simple examples, as well as a final example on which five hundred aggregative semantics are tested and compared, illustrating the range of possible behaviours with aggregative semantics. Decomposing the computation into three distinct and interpretable steps leads to a more parametrisable computation: it keeps the bipolarity one step further than what is done in the literature, and it leads to more understandable gradual semantics.

### [14] [SAHOO: Safeguarded Alignment for High-Order Optimization Objectives in Recursive Self-Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06333)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着递归自我改进系统能力的增强，其输出可能出现微妙的对齐漂移，对系统安全性构成风险。

Method: SAHOO框架包含三个关键部分：(i) 目标漂移指数（GDI），一种结合语义、词汇、结构和分布特征的学习型多信号检测器；(ii) 约束保持检查，用于强制执行语法正确性和非幻觉等安全关键不变性；(iii) 回归风险量化，用于标记可能撤销先前改进的优化周期。

Result: 在代码生成、数学推理和真实性等189个任务上，SAHOO带来了显著的质量提升（代码任务提升18.3%，推理任务提升16.8%），在两个领域保持了约束，并在真实性方面保持了低违规率。此外，研究还绘制了能力-对齐的边界，揭示了早期改进的效率和后期对齐成本的增加，以及像流畅性与事实性等领域特定的权衡。

Conclusion: SAHOO框架使得递归自我改进过程中的对齐保持变得可衡量、可部署和可扩展地系统验证，有效地解决了对齐漂移问题。

Abstract: Recursive self-improvement is moving from theory to practice: modern systems can critique, revise, and evaluate their own outputs, yet iterative self-modification risks subtle alignment drift. We introduce SAHOO, a practical framework to monitor and control drift through three safeguards: (i) the Goal Drift Index (GDI), a learned multi-signal detector combining semantic, lexical, structural, and distributional measures; (ii) constraint preservation checks that enforce safety-critical invariants such as syntactic correctness and non-hallucination; and (iii) regression-risk quantification to flag improvement cycles that undo prior gains. Across 189 tasks in code generation, mathematical reasoning, and truthfulness, SAHOO produces substantial quality gains, including 18.3 percent improvement in code tasks and 16.8 percent in reasoning, while preserving constraints in two domains and maintaining low violations in truthfulness. Thresholds are calibrated on a small validation set of 18 tasks across three cycles. We further map the capability-alignment frontier, showing efficient early improvement cycles but rising alignment costs later and exposing domain-specific tensions such as fluency versus factuality. SAHOO therefore makes alignment preservation during recursive self-improvement measurable, deployable, and systematically validated at scale.

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为“模式门控编排”的方法，以解决大型语言模型（LLMs）在科学工作流程中引入的不确定性问题。该方法通过引入执行模式作为工作流程的强制性边界，确保了执行的确定性和可控性，同时仍允许一定的对话灵活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 研究认为，模式门控架构通过分离对话和执行权限，能够解耦灵活性和确定性之间的权衡。提出了三个操作原则——执行前澄清、约束性计划-执行编排以及从工具到工作流级别的门控——来指导模式门控编排的应用。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can now translate a researcher's plain-language goal into executable computation, yet scientific workflows demand determinism, provenance, and governance that are difficult to guarantee when an LLM decides what runs. We propose schema-gated orchestration as the resolving principle: the schema becomes a mandatory execution boundary at the composed-workflow level, so that nothing runs unless the complete action--including cross-step dependencies--validates against a machine-checkable specification.
  We operationalize the 2 requirements as execution determinism (ED) and conversational flexibility (CF), and use these axes to review 20 systems spanning 5 architectural groups along a validation-scope spectrum.   The resulting landscape reveals an empirical Pareto front--no reviewed system achieves both high flexibility and high determinism--but a convergence zone emerges between the generative and workflow-centric extremes. We argue that a schema-gated architecture, separating conversational from execution authority, is positioned to decouple this trade-off, and distill 3 operational principles--clarification-before-execution, constrained plan-act orchestration, and tool-to-workflow-level gating--to guide adoption.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度强化学习代理存在目标不对齐的问题，容易过早地利用早期奖励信号。虽然符号方法可以解决这个问题，但它们难以扩展且不适用于连续环境。因此，需要一种能够结合符号结构和深度策略优势的混合方法。

Method: 提出了一种两阶段的混合式分层强化学习（H^2RL）框架。第一阶段使用基于逻辑选项的预训练策略，引导代理学习目标导向的行为，避免短期奖励陷阱。第二阶段允许代理通过标准的与环境交互来进一步优化其策略。

Result: H^2RL 方法在长期决策任务上表现出色，并且代理的性能优于强大的纯神经网络、纯符号以及神经-符号混合基线方法。

Conclusion: H^2RL 是一种有效的混合方法，能够将符号结构注入到深度强化学习代理中，在不牺牲深度策略表现力的同时，解决目标不对齐问题，并在长期决策任务中取得显著的性能提升。

Abstract: Deep reinforcement learning agents are often misaligned, as they over-exploit early reward signals. Recently, several symbolic approaches have addressed these challenges by encoding sparse objectives along with aligned plans. However, purely symbolic architectures are complex to scale and difficult to apply to continuous settings. Hence, we propose a hybrid approach, inspired by humans' ability to acquire new skills. We use a two-stage framework that injects symbolic structure into neural-based reinforcement learning agents without sacrificing the expressivity of deep policies. Our method, called Hybrid Hierarchical RL (H^2RL), introduces a logical option-based pretraining strategy to steer the learning policy away from short-term reward loops and toward goal-directed behavior while allowing the final policy to be refined via standard environment interaction. Empirically, we show that this approach consistently improves long-horizon decision-making and yields agents that outperform strong neural, symbolic, and neuro-symbolic baselines.

</details>

### [17] [Thinking with Spatial Code for Physical-World Video Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05591)
*Jieneng Chen,Wenxin Ma,Ruisheng Yuan,Yunzhi Zhang,Jiajun Wu,Alan Yuille*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Thinking with Spatial Code的框架，将RGB视频转换为显式的、时间连贯的3D表示，用于物理世界视觉问答。该框架能够使大型语言模型（LLMs）直接推理显式的空间变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了使大型语言模型（LLMs）能够直接处理和推理物理世界中的3D视觉信息，需要一种将视频转化为显式、时间连贯的3D表示的方法。

Method: 提出了一个空间编码器，通过融合6D物体解析和跟踪主干以及几何预测，将图像和几何特征编码成具有显式3D定向边界框和语义标签的结构化空间代码。此外，使用基于空间评估标准的奖励信号（spatial rubric reward）通过强化学习对LLMs进行微调，鼓励具有视角感知和几何基础的推理。

Result: 所提出的模型在VSI-Bench基准上优于专有的视觉-语言模型，达到了新的最先进水平。

Conclusion: Thinking with Spatial Code框架能够有效地将视频转化为3D表示，并使LLMs能够进行更精确的3D推理，从而在物理世界视觉问答任务上取得优异表现。

Abstract: We introduce Thinking with Spatial Code, a framework that transforms RGB video into explicit, temporally coherent 3D representations for physical-world visual question answering. We highlight the empirical finding that our proposed spatial encoder can parse videos into structured spatial code with explicit 3D oriented bounding boxes and semantic labels, enabling large language models (LLMs) to reason directly over explicit spatial variables. Specifically, we propose the spatial encoder that encodes image and geometric features by unifying 6D object parsing and tracking backbones with geometric prediction, and we further finetuning LLMs with reinforcement learning using a spatial rubric reward that encourages perspective-aware, geometrically grounded inference. As a result, our model outperforms proprietary vision-language models on VSI-Bench, setting a new state-of-the-art. Code is available at https://github.com/Beckschen/spatialcode.

### [18] [Adversarial Batch Representation Augmentation for Batch Correction in High-Content Cellular Screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05622)
*Lei Tong,Xujing Yao,Adam Corrigan,Long Chen,Navin Rathna Kumar,Kerry Hallbrook,Jonathan Orme,Yinhai Wang,Huiyu Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为ABRA（Adversarial Batch Representation Augmentation）的方法，通过将生物批次效应建模为领域泛化问题，并采用对抗性生成最差情况的批次扰动，从而在不依赖额外先验知识的情况下，显著提高了深度学习模型在细胞成像数据上的泛化能力，并在大规模数据集上取得了最先进的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的高内涵筛选技术产生了大量的细胞成像数据，但实验批次差异（bio-batch effects）会导致数据分布偏移，降低深度学习模型在未见过数据上的泛化能力。现有批次校正方法通常需要额外信息或难以泛化到新的生物批次。

Method: 将生物批次效应缓解视为领域泛化（DG）问题，提出ABRA方法。ABRA通过将特征统计量参数化为结构化不确定性来显式建模批次统计波动，并利用对抗性训练框架在表示空间中生成最差的生物批次扰动，同时保持类别的可辨别性。为了防止表示崩溃，还引入了协同分布对齐目标。

Result: 在RxRx1和RxRx1-WILDS基准数据集上的广泛评估表明，ABRA在siRNA扰动分类任务上达到了新的最先进水平。

Conclusion: ABRA是一种有效的方法，可以将生物批次效应的缓解视为领域泛化问题，通过对抗性生成和结构化不确定性来提高深度学习模型在细胞成像数据上的泛化能力，尤其在siRNA扰动分类任务上表现出色。

Abstract: High-Content Screening routinely generates massive volumes of cell painting images for phenotypic profiling. However, technical variations across experimental executions inevitably induce biological batch (bio-batch) effects. These cause covariate shifts and degrade the generalization of deep learning models on unseen data. Existing batch correction methods typically rely on additional prior knowledge (e.g., treatment or cell culture information) or struggle to generalize to unseen bio-batches. In this work, we frame bio-batch mitigation as a Domain Generalization (DG) problem and propose Adversarial Batch Representation Augmentation (ABRA). ABRA explicitly models batch-wise statistical fluctuations by parameterizing feature statistics as structured uncertainties. Through a min-max optimization framework, it actively synthesizes worst-case bio-batch perturbations in the representation space, guided by a strict angular geometric margin to preserve fine-grained class discriminability. To prevent representation collapse during this adversarial exploration, we introduce a synergistic distribution alignment objective. Extensive evaluations on the large-scale RxRx1 and RxRx1-WILDS benchmarks demonstrate that ABRA establishes a new state-of-the-art for siRNA perturbation classification.

### [19] [DreamCAD: Scaling Multi-modal CAD Generation using Differentiable Parametric Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05607)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的计算机辅助设计（CAD）生成方法受限于小规模、带有显式设计历史或边界表示（BRep）标签的标注数据集，而大量的未标注3D网格数据未能被有效利用，阻碍了CAD生成的可扩展性。研究者希望开发一种能够利用无标注3D数据生成可编辑BRep的方法。

Method: DreamCAD将BRep表示为一组参数化曲面（如Bézier曲面），并采用可微分的镶嵌方法生成网格。这种方法允许在大规模3D数据集上进行训练，同时重构出连接且可编辑的曲面。此外，研究者创建了CADCap-1M数据集，使用GPT-5生成了100万条文本描述，以促进文本到CAD的研究。

Result: DreamCAD在ABC和Objaverse基准测试中，在文本、图像和点云模态下均达到了最先进的性能。该方法提高了几何保真度，并且在用户偏好测试中获得了超过75%的优势。

Conclusion: DreamCAD成功地实现了从点云数据直接生成可编辑BRep，克服了对CAD特定标注数据的依赖，并能够利用大规模无标注3D数据进行训练。结合CADCap-1M数据集，该框架在CAD生成任务中展现出强大的能力和广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Computer-Aided Design (CAD) relies on structured and editable geometric representations, yet existing generative methods are constrained by small annotated datasets with explicit design histories or boundary representation (BRep) labels. Meanwhile, millions of unannotated 3D meshes remain untapped, limiting progress in scalable CAD generation. To address this, we propose DreamCAD, a multi-modal generative framework that directly produces editable BReps from point-level supervision, without CAD-specific annotations. DreamCAD represents each BRep as a set of parametric patches (e.g., Bézier surfaces) and uses a differentiable tessellation method to generate meshes. This enables large-scale training on 3D datasets while reconstructing connected and editable surfaces. Furthermore, we introduce CADCap-1M, the largest CAD captioning dataset to date, with 1M+ descriptions generated using GPT-5 for advancing text-to-CAD research. DreamCAD achieves state-of-the-art performance on ABC and Objaverse benchmarks across text, image, and point modalities, improving geometric fidelity and surpassing 75% user preference. Code and dataset will be publicly available.

</details>


### [20] [From Decoupled to Coupled: Robustness Verification for Learning-based Keypoint Detection with Joint Specifications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05604)
*Xusheng Luo,Changliu Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于热图关键点检测器的耦合鲁棒性验证框架，通过混合整数线性规划（MILP）来共同约束所有关键点的偏差，克服了现有解耦方法的局限性，并在严格误差阈值下展现出更高的验证率和有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关键点检测器对输入扰动敏感，但针对其进行形式化鲁棒性验证的研究很少，主要是因为输入高维和输出坐标连续。现有方法倾向于解耦验证，忽略了关键点之间的相互依赖性，导致验证结果过于保守。

Method: 提出了一种耦合鲁棒性验证框架，将问题建模为使用混合整数线性规划（MILP）进行证否（falsification）。该方法结合了可达热图集（reachable heatmap sets）和多面体（polytope）编码的联合偏差约束，共同验证所有关键点的行为。

Result: 实验证明，该耦合方法在验证率上优于解耦方法，尤其是在严格的误差阈值下，解耦方法失效时，该方法依然有效。当MILP无可行解时，证明模型鲁棒；当有可行解时，提供反例。

Conclusion: 所提出的耦合鲁棒性验证框架是首个能够共同约束关键点之间相互依赖性的验证方法，能够提供更精确的鲁棒性保证，并有效解决热图关键点检测器的鲁棒性验证问题。

Abstract: Keypoint detection underpins many vision tasks, including pose estimation, viewpoint recovery, and 3D reconstruction, yet modern neural models remain vulnerable to small input perturbations. Despite its importance, formal robustness verification for keypoint detectors is largely unexplored due to high-dimensional inputs and continuous coordinate outputs. We propose the first coupled robustness verification framework for heatmap-based keypoint detectors that bounds the joint deviation across all keypoints, capturing their interdependencies and downstream task requirements. Unlike prior decoupled, classification-style approaches that verify each keypoint independently and yield conservative guarantees, our method verifies collective behavior. We formulate verification as a falsification problem using a mixed-integer linear program (MILP) that combines reachable heatmap sets with a polytope encoding joint deviation constraints. Infeasibility certifies robustness, while feasibility provides counterexamples, and we prove the method is sound: if it certifies the model as robust, then the keypoint detection model is guaranteed to be robust. Experiments show that our coupled approach achieves high verified rates and remains effective under strict error thresholds where decoupled methods fail.

</details>


### [21] [Edges Are All You Need: Robust Gait Recognition via Label-Free Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05537)
*Chao Zhang,Zhuang Zheng,Ruixin Li,Zhanyong Mei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SKETCH的新型步态识别视觉模态，它通过边缘检测提取高频结构信息，无需语义标签。在此基础上，设计了一个名为SKETCHGAIT的多模态框架，结合SKETCH和传统的标签引导解析，并通过实验证明了其有效性，在SUSTech1K和CCPG数据集上取得了优异的识别性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有步态识别方法主要依赖轮廓和解析表示。轮廓信息稀疏，缺乏内部结构细节；解析方法依赖上游的人体解析器，性能不稳定。作者希望探索一种新的表示方法，能够捕捉更丰富的结构信息，并解决现有方法的局限性。

Method: 1. 提出SKETCH模态：通过边缘检测器从RGB图像中提取高频结构线索（如肢体关节和自遮挡轮廓），实现标签无关的结构信息提取。2. 设计SKETCHGAIT框架：一个层次解耦的多模态框架，包含两个独立流分别学习SKETCH和解析模态，并引入一个轻量级早期融合分支来捕捉两种模态的结构互补性。

Result: 在SUSTech1K数据集上，SKETCHGAIT达到了92.9%的Rank-1准确率；在CCPG数据集上，达到了93.1%的平均Rank-1准确率。实验证明了SKETCH模态的有效性以及SKETCHGAIT框架在融合不同模态信息方面的优势。

Conclusion: SKETCH是一种有效的步态识别视觉模态，能够提取丰富的结构信息而无需语义标签。SKETCHGAIT框架通过有效融合SKETCH和解析模态，克服了现有方法的局限性，显著提升了步态识别的性能。

Abstract: Gait recognition is a non-intrusive biometric technique for security applications, yet existing studies are dominated by silhouette- and parsing-based representations. Silhouettes are sparse and miss internal structural details, limiting discriminability. Parsing enriches silhouettes with part-level structures, but relies heavily on upstream human parsers (e.g., label granularity and boundary precision), leading to unstable performance across datasets and sometimes even inferior results to silhouettes. We revisit gait representations from a structural perspective and describe a design space defined by edge density and supervision form: silhouettes use sparse boundary edges with weak single-label supervision, while parsing uses denser cues with strong semantic priors. In this space, we identify an underexplored paradigm: dense part-level structure without explicit semantic labels, and introduce SKETCH as a new visual modality for gait recognition. Sketch extracts high-frequency structural cues (e.g., limb articulations and self-occlusion contours) directly from RGB images via edge-based detectors in a label-free manner. We further show that label-guided parsing and label-free sketch are semantically decoupled and structurally complementary. Based on this, we propose SKETCHGAIT, a hierarchically disentangled multi-modal framework with two independent streams for modality-specific learning and a lightweight early-stage fusion branch to capture structural complementarity. Extensive experiments on SUSTech1K and CCPG validate the proposed modality and framework: SketchGait achieves 92.9% Rank-1 on SUSTech1K and 93.1% mean Rank-1 on CCPG.

</details>


### [22] [Post Fusion Bird's Eye View Feature Stabilization for Robust Multimodal 3D Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05623)
*Trung Tien Dong,Dev Thakkar,Arman Sargolzaei,Xiaomin Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Post Fusion Stabilizer (PFS) 的轻量级模块，用于稳定自动驾驶中的相机-激光雷达融合BEV检测器的特征，以提高其在领域迁移和传感器故障下的鲁棒性，且易于集成到现有系统中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的相机-激光雷达融合BEV检测器在领域迁移和传感器故障下性能会显著下降，这限制了其在实际部署中的可靠性。现有的鲁棒性方法难以集成到已部署的系统中。

Method: 提出Post Fusion Stabilizer (PFS) 模块，该模块在现有检测器的中间BEV表示上操作，通过稳定特征统计、抑制传感器退化区域和通过残差校正恢复减弱的线索来稳定特征。PFS设计为接近同一变换，以保持性能并提高鲁棒性。

Result: PFS在nuScenes基准测试中，在相机丢弃鲁棒性方面提高了+1.2% mAP，在弱光性能方面提高了+4.4% mAP，同时参数量仅为3.3M，实现了最先进的性能。

Conclusion: PFS是一种轻量级的后融合稳定模块，能够有效提高相机-激光雷达融合BEV检测器在领域迁移和传感器故障下的鲁棒性，同时易于集成且不牺牲原有性能。

Abstract: Camera-LiDAR fusion is widely used in autonomous driving to enable accurate 3D object detection. However, bird's-eye view (BEV) fusion detectors can degrade significantly under domain shift and sensor failures, limiting reliability in real-world deployment. Existing robustness approaches often require modifying the fusion architecture or retraining specialized models, making them difficult to integrate into already deployed systems.
  We propose a Post Fusion Stabilizer (PFS), a lightweight module that operates on intermediate BEV representations of existing detectors and produces a refined feature map for the original detection head. The design stabilizes feature statistics under domain shift, suppresses spatial regions affected by sensor degradation, and adaptively restores weakened cues through residual correction. Designed as a near-identity transformation, PFS preserves performance while improving robustness under diverse camera and LiDAR corruptions. Evaluations on the nuScenes benchmark demonstrate that PFS achieves state-of-the-art results in several failure modes, notably improving camera dropout robustness by +1.2% and low-light performance by +4.4% mAP while maintaining a lightweight footprint of only 3.3 M parameters.

### [23] [Rethinking Concept Bottleneck Models: From Pitfalls to Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05629)
*Merve Tapli,Quentin Bouniot,Wolfgang Stammer,Zeynep Akata,Emre Akbas*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了CBM-Suite，一个用于解决概念瓶颈模型（CBM）局限性的方法框架，包括概念相关性度量、解决线性问题、缩小精度差距以及研究不同视觉骨干和视觉语言模型（VLMs）的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CBM存在概念相关性度量缺失、线性问题导致模型绕过概念瓶颈、精度与不透明模型差距大以及缺乏对视觉骨干和VLMs影响的系统研究等局限性。

Method: 1. 提出基于熵的概念集适用性度量。2. 在概念激活与分类器之间插入非线性层解决线性问题。3. 利用线性教师探测器引导的蒸馏损失缩小精度差距。4. 全面分析不同视觉编码器、VLMs和概念集对精度和可解释性的影响。

Result: CBM-Suite提高了模型的准确性，并为改进基于概念的可解释性提供了见解。

Conclusion: CBM-Suite是一个系统性的方法框架，有效解决了CBM面临的关键挑战，提高了模型的准确性和可解释性。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) ground predictions in human-understandable concepts but face fundamental limitations: the absence of a metric to pre-evaluate concept relevance, the "linearity problem" causing recent CBMs to bypass the concept bottleneck entirely, an accuracy gap compared to opaque models, and finally the lack of systematic study on the impact of different visual backbones and VLMs. We introduce CBM-Suite, a methodological framework to systematically addresses these challenges. First, we propose an entropy-based metric to quantify the intrinsic suitability of a concept set for a given dataset. Second, we resolve the linearity problem by inserting a non-linear layer between concept activations and the classifier, which ensures that model accuracy faithfully reflects concept relevance. Third, we narrow the accuracy gap by leveraging a distillation loss guided by a linear teacher probe. Finally, we provide comprehensive analyses on how different vision encoders, vision-language models, and concept sets interact to influence accuracy and interpretability in CBMs. Extensive evaluations show that CBM-Suite yields more accurate models and provides insights for improving concept-based interpretability.

</details>


### [24] [Making Reconstruction FID Predictive of Diffusion Generation FID](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05630)
*Tongda Xu,Mingwei He,Shady Abu-Hussein,Jose Miguel Hernandez-Lobato,Haotian Zhang,Kai Zhao,Chao Zhou,Ya-Qin Zhang,Yan Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为iFID的新指标，旨在解决现有rFID与扩散模型生成FID（gFID）相关性差的问题。iFID通过在潜在空间中进行插值来计算，并证明了其与gFID具有强相关性，同时解释了其有效性和rFID相关性差的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VAE重建FID（rFID）与潜在扩散模型的生成FID（gFID）之间存在相关性差的问题，这使得rFID无法有效地评估扩散模型的生成质量。

Method: 1. 提出iFID指标：对于数据集中每个样本，检索其在潜在空间中的最近邻（NN），然后插值它们的潜在表示。2. 解码插值后的潜在表示，并计算解码样本与原始数据集之间的FID。3. 分析rFID和iFID与扩散模型采样质量的关系，并解释iFID为何与gFID相关，以及rFID为何与gFID负相关。

Result: iFID首次实现了与扩散模型gFID的强相关性，其Pearson线性相关系数和Spearman秩相关系数均达到约0.85。研究还表明，rFID与扩散模型精炼阶段的样本质量相关，而iFID与扩散模型导航阶段的样本质量相关。

Conclusion: iFID是一种能够有效预测潜在扩散模型生成质量的新指标，解决了rFID与gFID相关性差的问题，并提供了理论解释。该研究的代码已公开。

Abstract: It is well known that the reconstruction FID (rFID) of a VAE is poorly correlated with the generation FID (gFID) of a latent diffusion model. We propose interpolated FID (iFID), a simple variant of rFID that exhibits a strong correlation with gFID. Specifically, for each element in the dataset, we retrieve its nearest neighbor (NN) in the latent space and interpolate their latent representations. We then decode the interpolated latent and compute the FID between the decoded samples and the original dataset. Additionally, we refine the claim that rFID correlates poorly with gFID, by showing that rFID correlates with sample quality in the diffusion refinement phase, whereas iFID correlates with sample quality in the diffusion navigation phase. Furthermore, we provide an explanation for why iFID correlates well with gFID, and why reconstruction metrics are negatively correlated with gFID, by connecting to results in the diffusion generalization and hallucination. Empirically, iFID is the first metric to demonstrate a strong correlation with diffusion gFID, achieving Pearson linear and Spearman rank correlations approximately 0.85. The source code is provided in https://github.com/tongdaxu/Making-rFID-Predictive-of-Diffusion-gFID.

</details>


### [25] [When Rubrics Fail: Error Enumeration as Reward in Reference-Free RL Post-Training for Virtual Try-On](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05659)
*Wisdom Ikezogwo,Mehmet Saygin Seyfioglu,Ranjay Krishna,Karim Bouyarmane*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为隐式误差计数（IEC）的新方法，用于在缺乏理想参考答案的场景下训练强化学习模型。IEC通过量化模型输出中的错误及其严重程度来生成奖励信号，并通过案例研究表明其在虚拟试穿等任务上优于基于规则的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于奖励的方法（如RLVR和RaR）在没有清晰的正确性信号或存在多个有效输出的实际任务中效果不佳，因为它们依赖于理想的参考答案来生成评估标准。研究人员希望弥补这一“无参考”场景下的空白。

Method: 提出隐式误差计数（IEC）方法。IEC不检查模型输出的正确之处，而是枚举其错误之处，并根据错误严重程度和任务相关轴进行加权评分，最终将其转换为校准后的每方面奖励。为了保证训练稳定性，IEC采用了隐式评分发射和分组校准两个关键设计。

Result: 在案例研究虚拟试穿（VTO）任务中，IEC表现出色。提出的评估指标级联误差计数（CEC）能很好地反映人类偏好。在MDressBench基准测试上，IEC在CEC指标上优于RaR。在VITON-HD和DressCode数据集上，IEC在8个感知指标中的6个上与或优于六个基线模型。

Conclusion: 在缺乏理想答案的情况下，通过计算误差可以提供比构建评估规则更强的信号，IEC是一种有效的解决方案，尤其适用于评估输出具有多种有效变体的任务。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) and Rubrics as Rewards (RaR) have driven strong gains in domains with clear correctness signals and even in subjective domains by synthesizing evaluation criteria from ideal reference answers. But many real-world tasks admit multiple valid outputs and lack the single ideal answer that rubric generation depends on. We identify this reference-free setting as a gap in current post-training methods and propose Implicit Error Counting (IEC) to fill it. Instead of checking what a response gets right against a rubric, IEC enumerates what it gets wrong, applying severity-weighted scores across task-relevant axes and converting them into calibrated per-aspect rewards. We show that naïve explicit enumeration is too noisy for stable optimization, and that two design choices: implicit score emission and group calibration are necessary to make error counting a reliable reward. As a case study, we validate IEC on virtual try-on (VTO), a domain that is simultaneously too constrained for holistic scoring and too permissive for rubric-based evaluation: subtle garment errors are unacceptable, yet many output variations are correct. We introduce Cascaded Error Counting (CEC) as an evaluation metric, which tracks human preferences well (60% top-1 vs. 30% others), and curate Mismatch-DressCode (MDressBench), a benchmark with maximal attribute mismatch to stress-test reward designs. On MDressBench, IEC outperforms RaR across all metrics (CEC: 5.31 vs. 5.60 on flat references; 5.20 vs. 5.53 on non-flat). On VITON-HD and DressCode, IEC matches or surpasses six baselines on 6 of 8 perceptual metrics. These results suggest that when ideal answers are unavailable, counting errors provide a stronger signal than constructing rubrics.

</details>


### [26] [Keeping the Evidence Chain: Semantic Evidence Allocation for Training-Free Token Pruning in Video Temporal Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05663)
*Jiaqi Li,Shuntian Zheng,Yixian Shen,Jia-Hong Huang,Xiaoman Lu,Minzhe Ni,Yu Guan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 SemVID 的训练免费视频时序定位（VTG）剪枝框架，通过保留关键证据和跨帧连接性，能在显著减少计算量（使用12.5%的视觉Token）的同时，保持高精度（最高95.4% mIoU）和加速推理（最高5.8倍）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视频语言模型（VLM）在处理长视频时计算成本高昂，视频时序定位（VTG）尤其依赖边界信息和跨帧推理，直接应用通用剪枝方法会导致性能大幅下降。因此，需要针对VTG任务特点设计新的剪枝策略。

Method: SemVID 遵循两个VTG特有的剪枝原则：1. 证据保留（ER），保留查询相关的关键图像块，尤其是在事件边界附近。2. 连接性强度（CS），保持Token级别的跨帧连接性以聚合长距离证据。该框架首先根据查询相关性和帧间变化分配Token预算，然后选择三种类型的Token：对象Token（提供多样化的查询关键证据）、运动Token（捕捉有意义的过渡并作为跨帧中继）和上下文Token（维持场景连贯性）。

Result: 在VTG基准测试中，SemVID 取得了优异的准确率-效率权衡。在仅使用12.5%视觉Token的情况下，mIoU保持在95.4%，并实现了高达5.8倍的预填充推理加速。在同等Token预算下，SemVID 的性能 consistently 优于现有方法。

Conclusion: SemVID 是一种有效的训练免费剪枝框架，能够为VTG任务显著降低计算成本，同时保持甚至提升模型性能，为解决长视频处理的效率问题提供了新思路。

Abstract: Video Temporal Grounding (VTG) localizes the temporal boundaries of a query-relevant moment in long, untrimmed videos, making video-language-model (VLM) pipelines prohibitively expensive. While recent training-free visual token pruning has shown success in video question answering, naively applying these objectives to VTG often causes drastic degradation, as VTG crucially depends on boundary-sensitive evidence and cross-frame reasoning chains. We therefore identify two VTG-specific pruning principles: Evidence Retention (ER), which keeps query-critical patches especially around event boundaries, and Connectivity Strength (CS), which preserves token-level cross-frame connectivity for long-range evidence aggregation. Building on these insights, we propose SemVID, a training-free pruning framework that constructs a compact yet coherent token subset with complementary semantic roles. SemVID first allocates per-frame token budgets by balancing query relevance and inter-frame variation to avoid over-pruned segments, and then selects three types of tokens: object tokens for diverse query-critical evidence, motion tokens to capture meaningful transitions and serve as cross-frame relays, and a small set of context tokens for scene continuity. Extensive experiments on VTG benchmarks show that SemVID achieves a strong accuracy-efficiency trade-off, retaining up to 95.4% mIoU with only 12.5% visual tokens and delivering up to a 5.8x prefill speedup, consistently outperforming prior methods under the same budgets.

</details>


### [27] [OWL: A Novel Approach to Machine Perception During Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05686)
*Daniel Raviv,Juan D. Yepes*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为OWL的新型感知函数，它利用视觉运动线索（局部视觉逼近和刚体旋转）来解决运动中的3D感知问题，无需先验知识或显式测量，实现了3D映射和相机航向的增强，并能在没有环境或相机模型信息的情况下进行3D场景重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的3D感知方法在运动中面临挑战，需要显式的测量或先验知识。研究旨在提出一种直接从基础视觉运动线索中提取信息的方法，以简化和增强3D感知能力，特别是在缺乏环境或相机模型信息的情况下。

Method: OWL函数直接从两个基础视觉运动线索（局部视觉逼近和相对刚体旋转）中推导而来，每个点在每个时间点都有对应的线索值。它通过这些线索值表达了相机与3D点之间的相对瞬时方向范围和方向平移关系，而无需直接测量这些物理量。该方法采用基于像素的并行计算。

Result: OWL函数能够实现3D对象的几何不变性，并仅凭视觉运动线索就能进行比例尺3D场景重建。仿真表明，OWL能够有效增强和简化3D映射和相机航向等感知能力。

Conclusion: OWL提供了一种统一的、基于时间的分析方法，用于处理运动中的3D感知问题，它无需先验知识或显式测量，能够从原始视觉运动图像序列中提取信息，实现3D场景的比例尺重建，并可能对机器人、自主导航、自然感知以及行为心理学和神经功能的研究提供新的视角和应用。

Abstract: We introduce a perception-related function, OWL, designed to address the complex challenges of 3D perception during motion. It derives its values directly from two fundamental visual motion cues, with one set of cue values per point per time instant. During motion, two visual motion cues relative to a fixation point emerge: 1) perceived local visual looming of points near the fixation point, and 2) perceived rotation of the rigid object relative to the fixation point. It also expresses the relation between two well-known physical quantities, the relative instantaneous directional range and directional translation in 3D between the camera and any visible 3D point, without explicitly requiring their measurement or prior knowledge of their individual values. OWL offers a unified, analytical time-based approach that enhances and simplifies key perception capabilities, including scaled 3D mapping and camera heading. Simulations demonstrate that OWL achieves geometric constancy of 3D objects over time and enables scaled 3D scene reconstruction from visual motion cues alone. By leveraging direct measurements from raw visual motion image sequences, OWL values can be obtained without prior knowledge of stationary environments, moving objects, or camera motion. This approach employs minimalistic, pixel-based, parallel computations, providing an alternative real-time representation for 3D points in relative motion. OWL bridges the gap between theoretical concepts and practical applications in robotics and autonomous navigation and may unlock new possibilities for real-time decision-making and interaction, potentially serving as a building block for next-generation autonomous systems. This paper offers an alternative perspective on machine perception, with implications that may extend to natural perception and contribute to a better understanding of behavioral psychology and neural functionality.

</details>


### [28] [MultiHaystack: Benchmarking Multimodal Retrieval and Reasoning over 40K Images, Videos, and Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05697)
*Dannong Xu,Zhongyu Yang,Jun Chen,Yingfang Yuan,Ming Hu,Lei Sun,Luc Van Gool,Danda Pani Paudel,Chun-Mei Feng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究提出了MultiHaystack，一个评估多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在大规模异构多模态语料库中进行证据检索和推理的新基准。结果表明，现有模型在需要检索证据时性能显著下降，表明多模态检索是当前MLLMs面临的主要瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对MLLMs的基准测试仅评估单一模态的理解能力，未能反映现实世界中从大规模异构多模态语料库中检索相关证据 prior to reasoning 的关键需求。现有的检索设置过于简化，夸大了模型的端到端可靠性。

Method: 引入MultiHaystack基准，包含超过46,000个跨文档、图像和视频的多模态检索候选，以及747个开放且可验证的问题。每个问题都对应一个唯一的、经过验证的证据项，需要跨模态的证据定位和细粒度推理。

Result: 模型在提供对应证据时表现良好，但在需要从整个语料库中检索证据时性能急剧下降。最强的检索器E5-V的Recall@1仅为40.8%。最先进的MLLM（如GPT-5）在提供对应证据时推理准确率为80.86%，但在检索前5个结果后下降至51.4%。

Conclusion: 多模态异构语料库的检索是当前MLLMs面临的主要瓶颈。MultiHaystack是一个有价值的测试平台，能够揭示现有评估方法所掩盖的深层局限性，并推动多模态系统的检索能力发展。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) achieve strong performance on benchmarks that evaluate text, image, or video understanding separately. However, these settings do not assess a critical real-world requirement, which involves retrieving relevant evidence from large, heterogeneous multimodal corpora prior to reasoning. Most existing benchmarks restrict retrieval to small, single-modality candidate sets, substantially simplifying the search space and overstating end-to-end reliability. To address this gap, we introduce MultiHaystack, the first benchmark designed to evaluate both retrieval and reasoning under large-scale, cross-modal conditions. MultiHaystack comprises over 46,000 multimodal retrieval candidates across documents, images, and videos, along with 747 open yet verifiable questions. Each question is grounded in a unique validated evidence item within the retrieval pool, requiring evidence localization across modalities and fine-grained reasoning. In our study, we find that models perform competitively when provided with the corresponding evidence, but their performance drops sharply when required to retrieve that evidence from the full corpus. Additionally, even the strongest retriever, E5-V, achieves only 40.8% Recall@1, while state-of-the-art MLLMs such as GPT-5 experience a significant drop in reasoning accuracy from 80.86% when provided with the corresponding evidence to 51.4% under top-5 retrieval. These results indicate that multimodal retrieval over heterogeneous pools remains a primary bottleneck for MLLMs, positioning MultiHaystack as a valuable testbed that highlights underlying limitations obscured by small-scale evaluations and promotes retrieval-centric advances in multimodal systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的图像地理定位技术在处理视觉信息的模糊性和利用听觉线索的潜力方面存在挑战，因此需要更精确的全球地理定位方法。

Method: 提出一个三阶段的视听地理定位框架：1. 感知阶段：使用混合自回归稀疏自编码器分解音频为“声学原子”。2. 多模态推理阶段：使用通过GRPO微调的多模态大语言模型整合声学原子和视觉特征。3. 精准预测阶段：在$S^2$流形上使用黎曼流匹配进行预测。

Abstract: While recent advances in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have improved image-based localization, precise global geolocation remains a formidable challenge due to the inherent ambiguity of visual landscapes and the largely untapped potential of auditory cues. In this paper, we introduce Audiovisual Geolocation, a framework designed to resolve geographic ambiguity through interpretable perception and reasoning. We present AVG, a high-quality global-scale video benchmark for geolocation, comprising 20,000 curated clips across 1,000 distinct locations. To address the complexity of audiovisual geolocation, we propose a three-stage framework: (1) a Perception stage that utilizes a mixture-autoregressive sparse autoencoder to decompose noisy audio into semantically grounded "acoustic atoms"; (2) a Multimodal Reasoning stage that employs an MLLM finetuned via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to synthesize these atoms with visual features; and (3) a Precision Prediction stage using Riemannian Flow Matching on the $S^2$ manifold. Our experiments demonstrate that our framework significantly outperforms unimodal baselines. These results entail that interpretable perception of the soundscape provides a critical, orthogonal signal that, when coupled with multimodal reasoning, enables high-precision global localization.

Method: NOVA将3D轨迹重新定义为结构化的时空语义序列，同时编码物理运动连续性和语言先验。利用LLM的自回归能力，将跟踪任务转化为序列的下一步补全问题，通过语言空间层级结构解决语义模糊，并利用常识推理保持身份一致性。

To address this, we propose Next-step Open-Vocabulary Autoregression (NOVA), an innovative paradigm that shifts 3D tracking from traditional fragmented distance-based matching toward generative spatio-temporal semantic modeling. NOVA reformulates 3D trajectories as structured spatio-temporal semantic sequences, enabling the simultaneous encoding of physical motion continuity and deep linguistic priors. By leveraging the autoregressive capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), we transform the tracking task into a principled process of next-step sequence completion. This mechanism allows the model to explicitly utilize the hierarchical structure of language space to resolve fine-grained semantic ambiguities and maintain identity consistency across complex long-range sequences through high-level commonsense reasoning. Extensive experiments on nuScenes, V2X-Seq-SPD, and KITTI demonstrate the superior performance of NOVA. Notably, on the nuScenes dataset, NOVA achieves an AMOTA of 22.41% for Novel categories, yielding a significant 20.21% absolute improvement over the baseline. Method: Any2Full将深度补全重新定义为预训练单目深度估计模型的尺度提示适应。它引入了一个尺度感知提示编码器，将稀疏输入的尺度线索提炼成统一的尺度提示，指导单目深度估计模型进行全局尺度一致的预测，同时保留其几何先验。

Abstract: Accurate, dense depth estimation is crucial for robotic perception, but commodity sensors often yield sparse or incomplete measurements due to hardware limitations. Existing RGBD-fused depth completion methods learn priors jointly conditioned on training RGB distribution and specific depth patterns, limiting domain generalization and robustness to various depth patterns. Recent efforts leverage monocular depth estimation (MDE) models to introduce domain-general geometric priors, but current two-stage integration strategies relying on explicit relative-to-metric alignment incur additional computation and introduce structured distortions. To this end, we present Any2Full, a one-stage, domain-general, and pattern-agnostic framework that reformulates completion as a scale-prompting adaptation of a pretrained MDE model. To address varying depth sparsity levels and irregular spatial distributions, we design a Scale-Aware Prompt Encoder. It distills scale cues from sparse inputs into unified scale prompts, guiding the MDE model toward globally scale-consistent predictions while preserving its geometric priors. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Any2Full achieves superior robustness and efficiency. It outperforms OMNI-DC by 32.2\% in average AbsREL and delivers a 1.4$\times$ speedup over PriorDA with the same MDE backbone, establishing a new paradigm for universal depth completion. Codes and checkpoints are available at https://github.com/zhiyuandaily/Any2Full.

### [32] [Can we Trust Unreliable Voxels? Exploring 3D Semantic Occupancy Prediction under Label Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06279)

Method: 1. 建立OccNL基准，专门用于研究不对称和动态尾随噪声下的3D占用预测。2. 提出DPR-Occ框架，采用双源部分标签推理构建可靠监督。3. 结合时序模型记忆和表示级结构亲和性，动态扩展和剪枝候选标签集，以保留真实语义并抑制噪声传播。

Result: 在SemanticKITTI数据集上，DPR-Occ在极端噪声（高达90%）下表现出优越的性能，相比于现有标签噪声学习基线，在mIoU和IoU上分别取得了显著提升（最高2.57% mIoU和13.91% IoU），避免了几何和语义的崩溃。

Conclusion: OccNL基准和DPR-Occ框架为在动态环境中进行安全关键的机器人感知奠定了可靠基础，证明了在存在严重标签噪声的情况下，通过精心设计的鲁棒方法仍能实现可靠的3D语义占用预测。

Abstract: 3D semantic occupancy prediction is a cornerstone of robotic perception, yet real-world voxel annotations are inherently corrupted by structural artifacts and dynamic trailing effects. This raises a critical but underexplored question: can autonomous systems safely rely on such unreliable occupancy supervision? To systematically investigate this issue, we establish OccNL, the first benchmark dedicated to 3D occupancy under occupancy-asymmetric and dynamic trailing noise. Our analysis reveals a fundamental domain gap: state-of-the-art 2D label noise learning strategies collapse catastrophically in sparse 3D voxel spaces, exposing a critical vulnerability in existing paradigms. To address this challenge, we propose DPR-Occ, a principled label noise-robust framework that constructs reliable supervision through dual-source partial label reasoning. By synergizing temporal model memory with representation-level structural affinity, DPR-Occ dynamically expands and prunes candidate label sets to preserve true semantics while suppressing noise propagation. Extensive experiments on SemanticKITTI demonstrate that DPR-Occ prevents geometric and semantic collapse under extreme corruption. Notably, even at 90% label noise, our method achieves significant performance gains (up to 2.57% mIoU and 13.91% IoU) over existing label noise learning baselines adapted to the 3D occupancy prediction task. By bridging label noise learning and 3D perception, OccNL and DPR-Occ provide a reliable foundation for safety-critical robotic perception in dynamic environments. The benchmark and source code will be made publicly available at https://github.com/mylwx/OccNL.

### [37] [Layer-wise Instance Binding for Regional and Occlusion Control in Text-to-Image Diffusion Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05769)
*Ruidong Chen,Yancheng Bai,Xuanpu Zhang,Jianhao Zeng,Lanjun Wang,Dan Song,Lei Sun,Xiangxiang Chu,Anan Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LayerBind 提出了一种新颖的、无需训练的文本到图像生成方法，通过将区域生成视为独立层并控制其早期去噪阶段的融合，实现了精确的区域布局和遮挡顺序控制，适用于各种扩散 Transformer 模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: LayerBind 分为两个阶段：实例初始化和语义护理。实例初始化利用多模态联合注意力机制，为每个实例创建独立分支，并在早期去噪步骤中根据图层顺序融合，形成预设布局的统一潜空间。语义护理通过层级注意力增强和层透明度调度器，在标准全局路径之外引入序列化层级注意力路径，以细化区域细节和维持遮挡顺序。

Abstract: Region-instructed layout control in text-to-image generation is highly practical, yet existing methods suffer from limitations: (i) training-based approaches inherit data bias and often degrade image quality, and (ii) current techniques struggle with occlusion order, limiting real-world usability. To address these issues, we propose LayerBind. By modeling regional generation as distinct layers and binding them during the generation, our method enables precise regional and occlusion controllability. Our motivation stems from the observation that spatial layout and occlusion are established at a very early denoising stage, suggesting that rearranging the early latent structure is sufficient to modify the final output. Building on this, we structure the scheme into two phases: instance initialization and subsequent semantic nursing. (1) First, leveraging the contextual sharing mechanism in multimodal joint attention, Layer-wise Instance Initialization creates per-instance branches that attend to their own regions while anchoring to the shared background. At a designated early step, these branches are fused according to the layer order to form a unified latent with a pre-established layout. (2) Then, Layer-wise Semantic Nursing reinforces regional details and maintains the occlusion order via a layer-wise attention enhancement. Specifically, a sequential layered attention path operates alongside the standard global path, with updates composited under a layer-transparency scheduler. LayerBind is training-free and plug-and-play, serving as a regional and occlusion controller across Diffusion Transformers. Beyond generation, it natively supports editable workflows, allowing for flexible modifications like changing instances or rearranging visible orders. Both qualitative and quantitative results demonstrate LayerBind's effectiveness, highlighting its strong potential for creative applications.

Abstract: Dense image retrieval is accurate but offers limited interpretability and attribution, and it can be compute-intensive at scale. We present \textbf{BM25-V}, which applies Okapi BM25 scoring to sparse visual-word activations from a Sparse Auto-Encoder (SAE) on Vision Transformer patch features. Across a large gallery, visual-word document frequencies are highly imbalanced and follow a Zipfian-like distribution, making BM25's inverse document frequency (IDF) weighting well suited for suppressing ubiquitous, low-information words and emphasizing rare, discriminative ones. BM25-V retrieves high-recall candidates via sparse inverted-index operations and serves as an efficient first-stage retriever for dense reranking. Across seven benchmarks, BM25-V achieves Recall@200 $\geq$ 0.993, enabling a two-stage pipeline that reranks only $K{=}200$ candidates per query and recovers near-dense accuracy within $0.2$\% on average. ### [39] [Spectral Probing of Feature Upsamplers in 2D-to-3D Scene Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05787)
*Ling Xiao,Yuliang Xiu,Yue Chen,Guoming Wang,Toshihiko Yamasaki*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种新的2D转3D管道中的特征增强器评估框架，发现光谱结构的一致性比空间细节的增强对3D重建质量更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有2D转3D管道的特征增强方法主要关注空间细节，但对3D感知的影响被忽视，因此需要一种新的方法来评估特征增强器对3D重建的影响。

Method: 研究者提出了一个包含六个指标的光谱诊断框架，用于分析振幅重分布、结构光谱对齐和方向稳定性。在CLIP和DINO骨干网络上，对经典插值和可学习增强方法进行了评估。

Result: 研究发现了三个主要结果：1. 结构光谱一致性（SSC/CSC）是神经视图合成（NVS）质量的最佳预测指标，而高频光谱斜率漂移（HFSS）通常与重建性能负相关。2. 几何和纹理对不同的光谱属性敏感：角度能量一致性（ADC）与几何相关性更强，而SSC/CSC对纹理保真度的影响略大于几何精度。3. 可学习增强器虽然能产生更清晰的空间特征，但很少在重建质量上优于经典插值，且其有效性取决于重建模型。

Conclusion: 3D重建质量与保留光谱结构比增强空间细节更密切相关，这强调了光谱一致性是设计2D转3D管道中特征增强策略的一个重要原则。

Abstract: A typical 2D-to-3D pipeline takes multi-view images as input, where a Vision Foundation Model (VFM) extracts features that are spatially upsampled to dense representations for 3D reconstruction. If dense features across views preserve geometric consistency, differentiable rendering can recover an accurate 3D representation, making the feature upsampler a critical component. Recent learnable upsampling methods mainly aim to enhance spatial details, such as sharper geometry or richer textures, yet their impact on 3D awareness remains underexplored. To address this gap, we introduce a spectral diagnostic framework with six complementary metrics that characterize amplitude redistribution, structural spectral alignment, and directional stability. Across classical interpolation and learnable upsampling methods on CLIP and DINO backbones, we observe three key findings. First, structural spectral consistency (SSC/CSC) is the strongest predictor of NVS quality, whereas High-Frequency Spectral Slope Drift (HFSS) often correlates negatively with reconstruction performance, indicating that emphasizing high-frequency details alone does not necessarily improve 3D reconstruction. Second, geometry and texture respond to different spectral properties: Angular Energy Consistency (ADC) correlates more strongly with geometry-related metrics, while SSC/CSC influence texture fidelity slightly more than geometric accuracy. Third, although learnable upsamplers often produce sharper spatial features, they rarely outperform classical interpolation in reconstruction quality, and their effectiveness depends on the reconstruction model. Overall, our results indicate that reconstruction quality is more closely related to preserving spectral structure than to enhancing spatial detail, highlighting spectral consistency as an important principle for designing upsampling strategies in 2D-to-3D pipelines.

### [40] [Margin and Consistency Supervision for Calibrated and Robust Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05812)
*Salim Khazem*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为MaCS的正则化框架，通过联合施加logit空间间隔和局部预测稳定性，有效提升了深度视觉分类器的校准性和鲁棒性，同时保持或提高准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度视觉分类器虽然准确率高，但在校准性和分布变化下的鲁棒性方面表现不佳。

Method: MaCS框架通过两种方式增强交叉熵损失：1. 采用hinge-squared margin penalty强制正确类别和最强竞争类别之间保持目标logit间隔。2. 采用consistency regularizer最小化干净输入和轻微扰动视图之间的预测KL散度。

Result: MaCS在多个图像分类基准测试和不同骨干网络（CNN和Vision Transformers）上，持续改善了校准性（降低ECE和NLL），并提高了对常见腐败的鲁棒性，同时保持或提高了Top-1准确率。

Conclusion: MaCS是一种简单、与架构无关的正则化框架，通过增加分类间隔并降低局部敏感性，理论上可以改善泛化能力并提供可证明的鲁棒性半径界限。该方法无需额外数据、无需改变架构，且推断开销极小，可作为标准训练目标的有效替代品。

Abstract: Deep vision classifiers often achieve high accuracy while remaining poorly calibrated and fragile under small distribution shifts. We present Margin and Consistency Supervision (MaCS), a simple, architecture-agnostic regularization framework that jointly enforces logit-space separation and local prediction stability. MaCS augments cross-entropy with (i) a hinge-squared margin penalty that enforces a target logit gap between the correct class and the strongest competitor, and (ii) a consistency regularizer that minimizes the KL divergence between predictions on clean inputs and mildly perturbed views. We provide a unifying theoretical analysis showing that increasing classification margin while reducing local sensitivity formalized via a Lipschitz-type stability proxy yields improved generalization guarantees and a provable robustness radius bound scaling with the margin-to-sensitivity ratio. Across several image classification benchmarks and several backbones spanning CNNs and Vision Transformers, MaCS consistently improves calibration (lower ECE and NLL) and robustness to common corruptions while preserving or improving top-1 accuracy. Our approach requires no additional data, no architectural changes, and negligible inference overhead, making it an effective drop-in replacement for standard training objectives.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 事件相机因其稀疏激活和高时间分辨率的特性，在机器人和计算机视觉任务中越来越受欢迎，特别是在需要精确、低功耗的定位场景。现有的事件相机视觉定位方法需要进一步提升。

Result: EventGeM在多个基准数据集和光照条件下，在事件相机视觉定位任务上取得了最先进的性能，优于当前最佳方法。该方法支持实时运行，并已在真实的机器人平台上进行了在线定位的演示。

Conclusion: EventGeM是一种高效且性能优越的事件相机视觉定位方法，通过有效的全局和局部特征融合，在各种条件下都能实现高精度的定位，并适用于实时机器人应用。

Abstract: Dynamic vision sensors, also known as event cameras, are rapidly rising in popularity for robotic and computer vision tasks due to their sparse activation and high-temporal resolution. In this work, we present EventGeM, a state-of-the-art global to local feature fusion pipeline for event-based Visual Place Recognition. We use a pre-trained vision transformer (ViT-S/16) backbone to obtain global feature patch for initial match predictions embeddings from event histogram images. Local feature keypoints were then detected using a pre-trained MaxViT backbone for 2D-homography based re-ranking with RANSAC. For additional re-ranking refinement, we subsequently used a pre-trained vision foundation model for depth estimation to compare structural similarity between references and queries. Our work performs state-of-the-art localization when compared to the best currently available event-based place recognition method across several benchmark datasets and lighting conditions all whilst being fully capable of running in real-time when deployed across a variety of compute architectures. Under this unified framework, the 3D cognition graph ensures the physical plausibility and structural rationality of 3D generation. Moreover, we construct a validation subset based on the Marble World Labs. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our Cog2Gen3D significantly outperforms existing methods in both semantic fidelity and geometric plausibility.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: BlackMirror包含两个主要组件：MirrorMatch，用于对齐视觉模式和指令以检测语义偏差；MirrorVerify，用于评估这些偏差在不同提示下的稳定性，以区分真正的后门行为和良性响应。

Abstract: This paper investigates the challenging task of detecting backdoored text-to-image models under black-box settings and introduces a novel detection framework BlackMirror. Existing approaches typically rely on analyzing image-level similarity, under the assumption that backdoor-triggered generations exhibit strong consistency across samples. However, they struggle to generalize to recently emerging backdoor attacks, where backdoored generations can appear visually diverse. BlackMirror is motivated by an observation: across backdoor attacks, {only partial semantic patterns within the generated image are steadily manipulated, while the rest of the content remains diverse or benign. Accordingly, BlackMirror consists of two components: MirrorMatch, which aligns visual patterns with the corresponding instructions to detect semantic deviations; and MirrorVerify, which evaluates the stability of these deviations across varied prompts to distinguish true backdoor behavior from benign responses. BlackMirror is a general, training-free framework that can be deployed as a plug-and-play module in Model-as-a-Service (MaaS) applications. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate that BlackMirror achieves accurate detection across a wide range of attacks. Code is available at https://github.com/Ferry-Li/BlackMirror.

### [48] [RAC: Rectified Flow Auto Coder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05925)
*Sen Fang,Yalin Feng,Yanxin Zhang,Dimitris N. Metaxas*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为 Rectified Flow Auto Coder (RAC) 的新模型，用于替代传统的 VAE，它通过多步解码、双向推理和路径上的潜在变量校正来提升生成质量，同时显著降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了改进传统 VAE 在生成质量和计算效率上的不足，特别是解决重建-生成之间的差距。

Method: 提出 Rectified Flow Auto Coder (RAC) 模型，其核心思想是将 Rectified Flow 概念应用于 VAE。具体包括：1. 通过将解码器应用于流的时间步长来实现多步解码，形成可修正的直观解码路径。2. 利用时间反转实现解码器作为编码器的双向推理，从而减少近 41% 的参数量。3. 在生成过程中，模型可以在潜在变量路径上进行校正，以改善生成质量。

Result: RAC 在重建和生成任务上均超越了目前最先进的 VAE 模型。与 SOTA VAEs 相比，RAC 的计算成本降低了约 70%。

Conclusion: RAC 是一种比传统 VAE 更优越的生成模型，它通过多步解码、双向推理和潜在变量校正，在生成质量和计算效率上取得了显著的进步。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a Rectified Flow Auto Coder (RAC) inspired by Rectified Flow to replace the traditional VAE: 1. It achieves multi-step decoding by applying the decoder to flow timesteps. Its decoding path is straight and correctable, enabling step-by-step refinement. 2. The model inherently supports bidirectional inference, where the decoder serves as the encoder through time reversal (hence Coder rather than encoder or decoder), reducing parameter count by nearly 41%. 3. This generative decoding method improves generation quality since the model can correct latent variables along the path, partially addressing the reconstruction--generation gap. Experiments show that RAC surpasses SOTA VAEs in both reconstruction and generation with approximately 70% lower computational cost.

Abstract: Accurate tumor analysis is central to clinical radiology and precision oncology, where early detection, reliable lesion characterization, and pathology-level risk assessment guide diagnosis and treatment planning. *Yukun Qi,Pei Fu,Hang Li,Yuhan Liu,Chao Jiang,Bin Qin,Zhenbo Luo,Jian Luan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为PatchCue的新型基于图像块的视觉提示范式，用于增强视觉语言模型（VLM）的视觉推理能力，通过在图像块层面提取和利用视觉信息，并在两阶段训练中结合监督微调和强化学习，有效提升了模型在多项基准测试中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉语言模型（VLM）推理方法（如Chain-of-Thought）主要依赖文本信息，未能充分利用视觉线索。虽然现有方法尝试融入像素级视觉线索，但需要精确的空间定位，增加了学习复杂度。研究旨在提出一种更有效且符合人类感知习惯的视觉推理范式。

Method: 提出PatchCue范式，将图像分割成图像块（patches），并在图像块层面提取视觉线索。采用两阶段训练方法：第一阶段为冷启动监督微调，使模型能够输出图像块级别的提示；第二阶段为强化学习，利用过程监督的提示奖励来指导中间的视觉推理步骤。

Result: 在多个VLM和各种基准（包括视觉问答、复杂推理和文档理解）上的广泛实验表明，PatchCue能持续提升模型的整体性能。结果显示，图像块级别的提示优于像素级别的边界框和基于点的提示。

Conclusion: PatchCue提供了一种更有效且在认知上更匹配的视觉推理范式，通过在图像块层面集成视觉信息，显著增强了VLM的视觉推理能力。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved remarkable progress on a wide range of challenging multimodal understanding and reasoning tasks. However, existing reasoning paradigms, such as the classical Chain-of-Thought (CoT), rely solely on textual information and often underutilize important visual cues. While prior work has incorporated pixel-level visual cues, these representations require precise spatial localization, introducing additional learning complexity. To address this, we propose PatchCue, a novel patch-based visual cue paradigm designed to significantly enhance the visual reasoning capabilities of VLMs. By partitioning images into patches and representing cues at the patch level, PatchCue aligns better with human perceptual habits and leverages the patch-tokenized input of modern VLMs. We train VLMs using a two-stage approach: cold-start supervised fine-tuning to output patch-level cues, followed by reinforcement learning with a process-supervised cue reward that guides intermediate visual reasoning steps. Extensive experiments on multiple VLMs and diverse benchmarks, including general visual question answering, complex reasoning, and document understanding, demonstrate that PatchCue consistently improves overall model performance. Our results show that patch-level cues outperform both pixel-level bounding boxes and point-based cues, providing a more effective and cognitively aligned visual reasoning paradigm.

</details>

Among the approaches to improve FER tasks, this paper focuses on deep architecture with the attention mechanism. We propose a novel Masking idea to boost the performance of CNN in facial expression task. In this work, we propose a memory-augmented segmentation agent (MemSeg-Agent) that shifts adaptation from weight space to memory space, enabling few-shot learning, federated supervised learning, and test-time adaptation within a unified architecture. MemSeg-Agent conditions a fixed backbone with lightweight static, few-shot, and test-time working memories, which are dynamically composed by an agentic controller. ### [54] [Energy-Driven Adaptive Visual Token Pruning for Efficient Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05950)
*Jialuo He,Huangxun Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为E-AdaPrune的能量驱动自适应剪枝框架，通过分析视觉特征空间的奇异值谱来动态确定视觉Token的数量，从而在不增加额外参数的情况下，根据图像信息密度自适应地分配Token，加速视觉语言模型（VLMs），并在多项基准测试中展现出性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉Token缩减方法通常使用固定的Token预算，无法有效处理图像信息密度差异带来的问题，这限制了视觉语言模型（VLMs）的加速效率。因此，需要一种能够根据图像内容自适应调整Token数量的方法。

Method: 提出E-AdaPrune框架，该框架利用视觉特征空间的奇异值谱来确定Token预算。通过保留一定比例的谱能量，该方法能够为信息密集的图像分配更多Token，同时压缩信息冗余的图像，且无需引入额外的可学习参数。具体实现上，采用随机奇异值分解（RSVD）来限制计算开销。

Result: 在九个基准测试和三种LLaVA VLM（LLaVA-1.5-7B, LLaVA-1.5-13B, LLaVA-NeXT-8B）上进行了评估。在相同的平均Token预算下，E-AdaPrune平均性能提升高达0.6%，在MMVet推理任务上相对提升达到+5.1%。RSVD引入的额外延迟控制在每张图片8毫秒。

Conclusion: E-AdaPrune是一种有效的能量驱动自适应剪枝框架，能够根据图像信息密度自适应地调整视觉Token数量，从而在不显著增加计算开销的情况下，提高视觉语言模型的性能，尤其是在推理能力方面。该方法为实现更高效的VLMs提供了一种有前景的途径。

Abstract: Visual token reduction is critical for accelerating Vision-Language Models (VLMs), yet most existing approaches rely on a fixed budget shared across all inputs, overlooking the substantial variation in image information density. We propose E-AdaPrune, an energy-driven adaptive pruning framework that determines the token budget from the singular value spectrum of the visual features space. By preserving a certain proportion of spectral energy, our method allocates more tokens to information-dense scenes while aggressively compressing redundant ones, without introducing additional learnable parameters. We evaluate E-AdaPrune on nine benchmarks and three VLM backbones, LLaVA-1.5-7B, LLaVA-1.5-13B, and LLaVA-NeXT-8B. Under matched average token budgets, E-AdaPrune consistently yields an average improvement of up to 0.6\%, including a significant +5.1\% relative boost on the MMVet reasoning task. Using randomized singular value decomposition, the additional latency is limited to 8ms per image.

### [55] [CylinderSplat: 3D Gaussian Splatting with Cylindrical Triplanes for Panoramic Novel View Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05882)
